### [186] [ARCOL: Aspect Ratio Constrained Orthogonal Layout](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29618)
*Zainab Alsuwaykit,Yousef Rajeh,Alexandre Kouyoumdjian,Steve Kieffer,Dominik Engel,Sara Di Bartolomeo,Martin Nöllenburg,Ivan Viola*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: ARCOL是一种正交图布局算法，通过将纵横比约束集成到应力最小化和树重连阶段，实现对布局纵横比的显式控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有正交布局方法主要关注面积利用率、总边长度和弯曲最小化等质量指标，但缺乏对布局全局纵横比的控制。随着宽屏显示器、移动设备等不同纵横比设备的普及，需要能够控制布局纵横比的正交布局方法。

Method: 基于HOLA算法，在应力最小化阶段将纵横比作为软约束，引导节点位置朝向目标纵横比；在树重连阶段修改成本函数，优先选择改善纵横比的放置方案。

Result: 通过定量评估、用户研究和专家访谈，ARCOL能够在不同纵横比下生成平衡且空间高效的正交布局。

Conclusion: ARCOL成功解决了正交图布局中纵横比控制的问题，为适应不同显示设备提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Orthogonal graph layout algorithms aim to produce clear, compact, and readable network diagrams by arranging nodes and edges along horizontal and vertical lines, while minimizing bends and crossings. Most existing orthogonal layout methods focus primarily on quality criteria such as area usage, total edge length, and bend minimization. Explicitly controlling the global aspect ratio (AR) of the resulting layout is as of now unexplored. Existing orthogonal layout methods offer no control over the resulting AR and their rigid geometric constraints make adaptation of finished layouts difficult. With the increasing variety of aspect ratios encountered in daily life, from wide monitors to tall mobile devices or fixed-size interface panels, there is a clear need for aspect ratio control in orthogonal layout methods. To tackle this issue, we introduce Aspect Ratio-Constrained Orthogonal Layout (ARCOL). Building upon the Human-like Orthogonal Layout Algorithm (HOLA)~\cite{Kieffer2016}, we integrate aspect ratio at two different stages: (1) into the stress minimization phase, as a soft constraint, allowing the layout algorithm to gently guide node positions toward a specified target AR, while preserving visual clarity and topological faithfulness; and (2) into the tree reattachment phase, where we modify the cost function to favor placements that improve the AR. We evaluate our approach through quantitative evaluation and a user study, as well as expert interviews. Our evaluations show that ARCOL produces balanced and space efficient orthogonal layouts across diverse aspect ratios.

### [190] [GENIE: Gram-Eigenmode INR Editing with Closed-Form Geometry Updates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29860)
*Samundra Karki,Adarsh Krishnamurthy,Baskar Ganapathysubramanian*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种无需重新训练即可编辑隐式神经表示（INR）学习形状的方法，通过利用INR倒数第二层特征的Gram算子的变形特征模态来实现单次闭式更新。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 隐式神经表示（INRs）为几何建模提供了紧凑模型，但尚不清楚学习到的形状何时可以在不重新训练的情况下进行编辑。需要一种方法来确定哪些变形是可行的，并实现高效的单次编辑。

Method: 利用INR倒数第二层特征的Gram算子，提取变形特征模态，这些模态参数化SDF零水平集的可实现编辑族。推导出单次闭式更新公式，无需优化即可对INR进行几何编辑。

Result: 发现变形模态不仅取决于几何本身，还需要从足够丰富的采样分布中估计Gram算子才能可靠恢复。理论上精确描述了在这种单次更新下可行的变形集合，证明编辑在变形模态张成的空间内是适定的。

Conclusion: 该方法实现了对INR学习形状的单次闭式编辑，无需重新训练，为隐式神经表示的几何编辑提供了理论基础和实用工具。

Abstract: Implicit Neural Representations (INRs) provide compact models of geometry, but it is unclear when their learned shapes can be edited without retraining. We show that the Gram operator induced by the INR's penultimate features admits deformation eigenmodes that parameterize a family of realizable edits of the SDF zero level set. A key finding is that these modes are not intrinsic to the geometry alone: they are reliably recoverable only when the Gram operator is estimated from sufficiently rich sampling distributions. We derive a single closed-form update that performs geometric edits to the INR without optimization by leveraging the deformation modes. We characterize theoretically the precise set of deformations that are feasible under this one-shot update, and show that editing is well-posed exactly within the span of these deformation modes.

### [191] [Wildfire Suppression: Complexity, Models, and Instances](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29865)
*Gustavo Delazeri,Marcus Ritt*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 该论文研究野火抑制资源在时间上的分配问题，证明该问题是NP完全问题，提出新的混合整数规划方法，并创建基于物理的实例生成器进行基准测试。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Wildfires cause major losses worldwide, and the frequency of fire-weather conditions is likely to increase in many regions. We study the allocation of suppression resources over time on a graph-based representation of a landscape to slow down fire propagation. Our contributions are theoretical and methodological. First, we prove that this problem and related variants in the literature are NP-complete, including cases without resource-timing constraints. Second, we propose a new mixed-integer programming (MIP) formulation that obtains state-of-the-art results, showing that MIP is a competitive approach contrary to earlier findings. Third, showing that existing benchmarks lack realism and difficulty, we introduce a physics-grounded instance generator based on Rothermel's surface fire spread model. We use these diverse instances to benchmark the literature, identifying the specific conditions where each algorithm succeeds or fails.

*Hirish Chandrasekaran,Andreas Kloeckner*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 提出混合符号-数值方法生成递推关系，以O(n)成本计算径向对称格林函数的n阶导数，应用于QBX方法并开发了新的旋转基评估方法


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高阶格林函数导数在泰勒基快速多极子法、Barnes-Hut n体算法和QBX中至关重要，但现有方法计算成本高，需要更高效的导数计算方法

Method: 开发混合符号-数值程序生成递推关系，仅需知道格林函数所满足的PDE，即可实现O(n)成本计算n阶导数；应用于QBX时提出新的基于旋转的笛卡尔坐标系目标特定评估方法

Result: 算法具有可控的理论误差，新QBX方法比现有符号方法成本显著降低，数值实验验证了精度和成本优势

Abstract: High-order derivatives of Green's functions are a key ingredient in Taylor-based fast multipole methods, Barnes-Hut $n$-body algorithms, and quadrature by expansion (QBX). In these settings, derivatives underpin either the formation, evaluation, and/or translation of Taylor expansions. In this article, we provide hybrid symbolic-numerical procedures that generate recurrences to attain an $O(n)$ cost for the the computation of $n$ derivatives (i.e. $O(1)$ per derivative) for arbitrary radially symmetric Green's functions. These procedures are general--only requiring knowledge of the PDE that the Green's function solves. We show that the algorithm has controlled, theoretically-understood error. We apply these methods to the method of quadrature by expansion, a method for the evaluation of singular layer potentials, which requires higher-order derivatives of Green's functions. In doing so, we contribute a new rotation-based method for target-specific QBX evaluation in the Cartesian setting that attains dramatically lower cost than existing symbolic approaches. Numerical experiments support our claims of accuracy and cost.

### [193] [Enhanced Channel Estimation for Flexible Intelligent Metasurface-Aided Communication Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29098)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统刚性均匀平面阵列（UPA）在信道估计方面存在局限性，而柔性智能超表面能够通过动态调整表面形状来改善信道条件，从而提高信道估计精度和系统性能。

Method: 1. 针对FIM增强的上行通信系统，定制正交匹配追踪（OMP）方法进行信道估计；2. 通过优化FIM表面形状来最小化测量矩阵的列相干性，同时满足形变范围约束；3. 基于估计的到达方向（DOA）和信道增益，进一步研究FIM增强的下行MISO系统的信噪比改进。

These elements can not only transmit signals, but also adapt their displacements in a direction perpendicular to the FIM surface via an attached controller. In this paper, we consider the channel estimation problem for the uplink of an FIM-enhanced communication system via customizing the orthogonal matching pursuit (OMP) method. Specifically, we formulate an optimization problem of minimizing the column coherence of the measurement matrix by optimizing the FIM's surface shape, subject to the morphing range constraint. Based on the estimated direction of arrival (DOA) and channel gain, we further investigate the signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) improvement in the FIM-enhanced downlink multiple-input single-output (MISO) system. Numerical results demonstrate that an FIM significantly outperforms a conventional rigid uniform planar array (UPA), thereby showing that FIM can substantially improve channel estimation accuracy and achieve SNR improvement, even when using estimated channel parameters.

</details>


### [194] [A Structural Characterization of Cyclotomic Cosets with Applications to Affine-Invariant Codes and BCH Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29150)
*Xiongkun Zheng,Dabin Zheng,Xiaoqiang Wang,Mu Yuan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 仿射不变码因其丰富的代数结构和强大的理论性质而备受关注。本文旨在研究一类特殊的仿射不变码，其定义集由单个特定元素的分圆陪集的所有后代构成，以深化对这类码的参数分析。

Result: 得到了后代集大小的精确组合公式；推导了仿射不变码及其循环码的维数显式公式；建立了对偶码最小距离的下界；特别针对设计距离为δ=(b+1)q^{m-t-1}的窄义本原BCH码，给出了精确维数公式和改进的最小距离下界。

Conclusion: 本文结果扩展并锐化了多个已知结果，为BCH码及其对偶码的参数分析提供了更精细的工具，特别改进了窄义本原BCH码的参数估计。

Abstract: Affine-invariant codes have attracted considerable attention due to their rich algebraic structure and strong theoretical properties. In this paper, we study a family of affine-invariant codes whose defining set consists of all descendants of elements in the cyclotomic coset of a single specified element. Our main contributions are as follows. First, we establish a new combinatorial result that determines exactly the size of such descendant sets, which is of independent interest in the study of cyclotomic cosets. Second, using this result, we derive explicit formulas for the dimensions of the corresponding affine-invariant codes and their associated cyclic codes, and we establish lower bounds on the minimum distances of their duals. In particular, under appropriate parameter choices, these codes yield narrow-sense primitive BCH codes and their extended counterparts. For the special class of narrow-sense primitive BCH codes with designed distance $δ= (b+1)q^{m-t-1}$, where $1 \leq b \leq q-1$ and $0 \leq t \leq m-1$, we provide exact dimension formulas and an improved lower bound on the minimum distance. The results presented here extend and sharpen several previously known results, and provide refined tools for the parametric analysis of BCH codes and their duals.

### [195] [Finite Blocklength Covert Communication over Quasi-Static Multiple-Antenna Fading Channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29645)
*Changhong Liu,Jingjing Wang,Qiaosheng Zhang,Jinpeng Xu,Lin Zhou*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文研究了准静态多天线衰落信道下隐蔽通信的最优码的有限码长性能，分析了不同CSI可用性情况，揭示了多天线系统带来的显著空间分集增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 国际电信联盟白皮书呼吁在衰落信道上实现极高安全性和低延迟通信。低延迟要求对应准静态衰落模型，而高安全性可通过隐蔽通信实现。为响应ITU的号召，研究准静态多天线衰落信道下隐蔽通信的最优码的有限码长性能。

Method: 使用Kullback-Leibler散度作为隐蔽性度量，研究合法发射机和接收机CSI可用性的所有四种情况，假设看守者知道从合法发射机到自身的完美CSI。将准η邻域框架扩展到衰落信道，处理随机信道矩阵带来的挑战。对于可靠性分析，由于隐蔽性约束导致的功率消失，通过精细控制高阶项和利用隐蔽中断概率特性，改进了Yang等人的非隐蔽分析。

Result: 当码长为n时，一阶隐蔽速率满足平方根定律，以Θ(n^{-1/2})缩放，系数由合法用户和看守者信道矩阵的迹决定，二阶速率消失。与Yang等人的非隐蔽结果不同，合法用户的CSI可用性不影响隐蔽通信的有限码长性能。揭示了多天线系统为隐蔽通信提供的显著空间分集增益。

Conclusion: 在准静态多天线衰落信道下，隐蔽通信的一阶速率遵循平方根定律，CSI可用性不影响性能，多天线系统提供显著空间分集增益。研究扩展了准η邻域框架到衰落信道，为隐蔽通信的有限码长分析提供了理论框架。

Abstract: The white book released by the International Telecommunications Union (ITU) calls for extremely high-security and low-latency communication over fading channels. Under the low-latency requirement, the corresponding fading model is quasi-static fading while high-security can be achieved via covert communication. In response to the call of ITU, we study the finite blocklength performance of optimal codes for covert communication over quasi-static multi-antenna fading channels, under the covertness metric of Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence. In particular, we study all four cases regarding the availability of channel state information (CSI) for legitimate transmitter and receiver, and assume that the warden knows perfect CSI for the channel from the legitimate transmitter to itself. Specifically, we show that, when the blocklength is $n$, the first-order covert rate satisfies the square root law, scaling as $Θ(n^{-\frac{1}{2}})$ with the coefficient determined by the traces of the channel matrices of the legitimate users and the warden, and the second-order rate vanishes. In contrast to the non-covert result of Yang et al. (TIT, 2014), we show that CSI availability at the legitimate users does not affect the finite blocklength performance for covert communication. Furthermore, we reveal the significant spatial diversity gain provided by multiple-antenna systems for covert communication. For the covertness analysis, we extend the quasi-$η$-neighborhood framework to fading channels and address challenges arising from the random channel matrices. For the reliability analysis, due to the vanishing power imposed by the covertness constraint, we refine the non-covert analysis by Yang et al. (TIT, 2014), by carefully controlling higher-order terms and exploiting the properties of covert outage probability.

</details>


### [196] [Joint Identification and Sensing with Noisy Feedback: A Task-Oriented Communication Framework for 6G](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29649)
*Yaning Zhao,Holger Boche,Christian Deppe*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文研究了带噪声严格因果反馈的状态相关离散无记忆信道上的联合识别与感知(JIDAS)，推导了容量-失真函数的上下界，量化了噪声反馈下JIDAS的基本极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 面向任务的通信是6G系统的关键使能技术，其目标是支持决策和行动而非完整消息重建。从信息论角度看，识别(ID)码为此范式提供了自然抽象，使接收器能够测试是否发送了任务相关消息而无需解码整个消息。受反馈对ID的强烈影响以及通信感知一体化日益增长的兴趣驱动，本文研究了带噪声严格因果反馈的状态相关离散无记忆信道上的联合识别与感知。

Result: 推导了JIDAS在噪声反馈下的容量-失真函数的下界和上界。结果表明，噪声反馈会降低识别速率并增加感知失真。这些结果量化了噪声反馈下JIDAS的基本极限，并将现有的无噪声反馈特性作为特例恢复。

Conclusion: 本文建立了带噪声反馈的联合识别与感知的理论框架，推导的容量-失真界限为6G系统中面向任务的通信设计提供了理论基础。结果表明，噪声反馈会限制JIDAS性能，但通过适当的编码策略仍可实现识别与感知的联合优化。

Abstract: Task-oriented communication is a key enabler of emerging 6G systems, where the objective is to support decisions and actions rather than full message reconstruction. From an information-theoretic perspective, identification (ID) codes provide a natural abstraction for this paradigm by enabling receivers to test whether a task-relevant message was sent, without decoding the entire message. Motivated by the strong impact of feedback on ID and by the growing interest in integrated communication and sensing, this paper studies joint identification and sensing (JIDAS) over state-dependent discrete memoryless channels with noisy strictly causal feedback. The transmitter conveys identification messages while simultaneously estimating the channel state from the feedback signal. For both deterministic and randomized coding schemes, we derive lower and upper bounds on the capacity--distortion function. The results quantify the fundamental limits of JIDAS under noisy feedback and recover existing noiseless-feedback characterizations as special cases.

Abstract: This paper proposes an $α$-fair multistatic integrated sensing and communication (ISAC) framework for multi-user multi-input multi-output (MIMO)-orthogonal frequency division multiplexing (OFDM) systems, where communication users act as passive bistatic receivers to enable multistatic sensing. Unlike existing works that optimize aggregate sensing metrics and thus favor geometrically advantageous targets, we minimize the $α$-fairness utility over per-target Cramér--Rao lower bounds (CRLBs) subject to per-user minimum data rate and transmit power constraints. The resulting non-convex problem is solved via the Riemannian conjugate gradient (RCG) method with a smooth penalty reformulation. Simulation results validate the effectiveness of the proposed scheme in achieving a favorable sensing fairness--communication trade-off.

Abstract: We present a new general method for performing basic arithmetic in the finite field~$\mathbb{F}_p$ for any prime $p>2$ by using traditional binary operations over~$\mathbb{F}_2$. Our new approach is efficient and competitive with current state-of-art methods. ### [199] [Reducing Subpacketization in Device-to-Device Coded Caching via Heterogeneous File Splitting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29945)
*Xiang Zhang,Giuseppe Caire,Mingyue Ji*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 扩展PT框架至异构子包化，通过联合优化包大小、用户分组和多播发射机选择，在保持最优速率的同时最小化子包化水平，为特定参数构造新的D2D编码缓存方案


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于包类型(PT)的D2D编码缓存方案仅使用同质子包化，即所有包大小相同，这限制了在某些参数范围内子包化水平的进一步降低。需要扩展PT框架以支持异构子包化，允许不同类型包具有不同大小，从而在更广泛参数范围内实现子包化水平的优化

Method: 1. 扩展PT框架至异构子包化，在精细化类型分类下允许包大小随类型变化；2. 联合优化包大小、用户分组和多播发射机选择，在保持最优通信速率的同时最小化总体子包化水平；3. 基于异构PT框架，为参数(K, KM/N)=(2q+1, 2r)构造新的D2D编码缓存方案

Result: 提出的构造相比Ji-Caire-Molisch(JCM)缓存方案实现了子包化水平的常数因子降低，并补充了现有PT设计无法适用的参数范围

Conclusion: 异构PT框架扩展了D2D编码缓存方案的设计空间，通过允许包大小变化实现了更优的子包化水平优化，为特定参数范围提供了有效的解决方案

Abstract: The packet type (PT)-based framework~\cite{zhang2026taming} provides a systematic and principled approach to designing device-to-device (D2D) coded caching schemes that achieve reduced \sbp while preserving the optimal communication rate. However, existing PT designs rely exclusively on homogeneous \sbp, where all packets have an identical size regardless of their types. This restriction limits the achievable \sbp reduction in certain parameter regimes. In this paper, we extend the PT framework to \emph{heterogeneous} \sbp, allowing packet sizes to vary across types under a refined type classification. The packet sizes, in conjunction with user grouping and multicast transmitter selection, are jointly optimized to minimize the overall \sbp level while preserving the optimal rate. Based on the heterogeneous PT framework, we construct a new class of D2D coded caching schemes for $(K, KM/N)=(2q+1, 2r)$ with $q,r \in \mathbb{N}_+$, where $K,N$ and $M$ denote the number of users, files and cache memory size, respectively. The proposed construction achieves a constant-factor reduction in \sbp compared to the Ji-Caire-Molisch (JCM) caching scheme~\cite{ji2016fundamental} and complements existing PT designs that are not applicable in this parameter regime.
